A Laughing Matter 176

— Sea Guest

Wife: "Dear, why do you look so unhappy today when you came home?"

Husband: "That darn account book in the office has been killing me. It makes my head spin every day."

Wife: "Then why don't you ask the manager to give you some new account books?"

Criminal: "Officer, I didn't steal the chicken. I just brought it home yesterday to play a joke on the chicken's owner."

Judge: "Now I'm locking you up in prison for a week, just to play a joke on you."

Drunk (shouting loudly in the theater): "Old Wang, Old Wang!"

Staff: "You can't shout loudly in here."

Drunk: "I'm calling my friend."

Staff: "But you can't shout so loudly."

Drunk: "He won't hear me if I shout quietly. He's in Tianjin."

A: "How could you travel all over that huge Paris in just two days?"

B: "We divided the work. My son specialized in cafes and dance halls. My wife specialized in department stores and theaters. I myself specialized in museums and art galleries. In our dreams at night, we took turns touring the places we hadn't been to."

A: "Have you heard about Mr. C posting an advertisement looking for a wife?"

B: "I haven't heard. What was the result?"

A: "More than a dozen men wrote to him, willing to offer their wives unconditionally."

Characters Similar to Autumn Crickets and Autumn Swallows 177

— Inkstone Old Man

Peiping, 11th Special Dispatch: Someone from Shijiazhuang said that Yan Xishan in Huolu has dug a tunnel connecting three gates, with air vents on top covered with dry grass to blend in with the ground. I say this is similar to crickets after the Cold Dew season. Crickets fear the cold, so they dig holes in the ground, with two or three openings for both avoiding the cold and allowing air to circulate, as well as facilitating entry and exit. The entrance to the hole is often covered with dry grass. Moreover, crickets like to fight. When defeated, they flee into the hole and dare not come out. Yan today is very similar.

Another dispatch: Yan told Wang that if he couldn't maintain things within two weeks, they would go abroad together, and said that you and Chen (Gongbo), Zou, Xie, Tan, and Mao were all invited by me. Mao is fully responsible for the expenses of going abroad. Chen Gongbo advocated preparing airplanes and, if necessary, flying to Kulun and taking a boat to France via Vladivostok. I say this is similar to swallows after the Autumn Equinox, flocking to the sea. Swallows work hard, carrying mud to build nests. Unfortunately, once the opportunity is gone, even if they are reluctant to leave, they cannot. Thinking back to the double-perched kingfisher beams, whispering to each other, how happy they were. Once hastily flying away, how can they not feel the difference between then and now? Today, Yan, Wang, Chen, and others will inevitably take the plane together with their wives, entrusting themselves to foreign lands. Is it not similar to the autumn swallows perching on the kingfisher beams, leaving their old nests and flying to the sea?

Inkstone Old Man jokingly offers a poem: "The Autumn Equinox and Cold Dew seasons are approaching too closely. Crickets hibernate in caves, pitifully entering traps. Swallows fly over the sea, chirping silently. Humans and animals can learn from each other. Not releasing the butcher's knife, one eventually loses the great power. If only they regretted it in the beginning, it's a pity it's too late to argue."

Talking About Japanese Rice 178

— Yellow Shadow Dull

Japan is an industrial country in the Far East. It does not produce much agricultural product. Most of its people's rice is imported from other countries. Now suddenly a large amount of Japanese rice is being shipped to various countries for sale. How can we not be surprised? In fact, Japan having surplus rice to sell to other countries is also a first in history. There are two major reasons why Japan has surplus rice for sale this time. One is that for years, in order to maintain rice prices, it has accumulated too much rice. The other is that this year's harvest has been abundant, with the new rice crop being twice as large as in previous years. Therefore, under these circumstances, the Japanese authorities have decided to ship the surplus rice abroad for sale. According to the planned destination, it includes China, the Dutch East Indies, the Near East, England, Germany, and other countries. Since the news came out, Japanese rice merchants engaged in import and export have flocked to volunteer for transportation.

Moreover, Japanese merchants have various favorable conditions when transporting rice this time. Whether the Japanese rice can be sold to various countries is difficult to determine in advance. Therefore, the authorities have promised that if the rice merchants suffer losses, the government will bear the responsibility. The purpose of exporting Japanese rice is to maintain domestic rice prices and protect the interests of farmers. If there is too much rice, the price will inevitably fall. It can be seen that the Japanese government has been making efforts to encourage agriculture in recent years. The sales of Japanese rice are mostly in Java, with an annual capacity of 2,000,000 dan. As for those dependent on the Dutch East Indies, there are 4,000,000 dan. The Japanese government has now decided to increase import tariffs to resist the import of rice. This matter has a great impact on rice importers in Japan.

Regarding the United Kingdom, the various procedures for shipping rice have now been fully determined. Most of the rice shipped by the Japanese government this time is old rice stored in granaries for many years. When shipping it to various countries, there is no fixed price standard. The only purpose is to seek balance based on market prices in various countries. As for the losses suffered, no matter how large or small, they can be ignored. Therefore, in the end, the government will inevitably suffer heavy losses. The Japanese government currently has 2,600,000,020 dan of old rice. The amount to be exported this time is estimated at 3,000,000 dan, with old rice accounting for eight-tenths of it. Its low quality is conceivable. The first time Japan exported rice was in 1914, with only 130,000 dan. The last time was in 1928, with only 500,000 dan, and it was transported privately by merchants. Most of it was imported foreign rice that had been hoarded. Therefore, the amount transported this time is unprecedented, and it is not entirely pure Japanese rice.

Let Me Talk About Cheng Yanqiu 179

— Jiang Zhifan

Recently, I accompanied my old wife and granddaughter on a trip to Tonglu, boating on the Seven Li Tan and climbing Yan Ziling's Fishing Platform. I was deeply impressed in my old age. On the return trip, I passed through Shanghai and was invited by my fellow villagers Qu and Cheng to the Grand Stage to watch Yanqiu perform a play. That evening, they performed "Rainbow Seizing" and "Wu Family Slope." His expression was delicate, and the supporting actors Wang Shaolou and Furong Cao were also good. The audience has their own evaluation. Seeing many couplets hanging in front of the stage, a friend praised Yanqiu's beauty and said that all the couplets could be used. He asked me to write a couplet that was definitely masculine and explicitly embedded the words "Yanqiu." After a brief thought, I replied that it was possible. I recalled a geisha named Qiu Zi whom I met in Dongying twenty-six years ago. She was also very beautiful. So I improvised a couplet to tell him: "I regret bringing a beautiful wife, fearing that she will be captivated at first sight and dislike me from now on. Recalling Qiu Zi's beauty, I realized that the two are of different genders. Why only think of her?" My wife is already sixty years old. How can she be considered a beautiful wife? I don't know if the poem "beautiful wife" does not refer to youth and beauty but mainly to someone capable of fanning emotions. So why is my old wife not capable of it? My friend pointed to a plaque hanging in the box with the words "No Dan Doesn't Cheng's Tune." The best. I looked at its right. Both plaques were mediocre. Further to the right, there were four words that were very appropriate. These four words were posted high on the wall, saying "Partial Head Pain." It can be interpreted as the audience sitting in the main hall but slightly off-center, which causes discomfort in the brain and a headache. I asked the audience if this was true. (In response)

Record of Tianning Temple 180

— Chen Boying

Tianning Temple is one of the large temples in Jiangnan. The temple is located outside the east gate of Changzhou, covering hundreds of acres. There are more than a thousand monks. Entering the temple, it is impossible to visit it all in a few days. When asked how many rooms there are in the temple, some say there is a number in the thousands. Although exaggerated, no one knows the exact number. The temple has shops selling all kinds of goods. Nothing needs to be sought outside. The wok for cooking rice is cast in copper and is so deep that one person can stand in it. It is hung from the beam with a rope and raised and lowered with a pulley. The main hall is very tall and steep. Looking up, it seems to have no roof. The Buddha statue is also unusually great. Legend has it that there is a gourd on the ridge of the hall, cast in pure copper, which can prevent wind and dust from affecting the area within two miles. The temple is rich. Jiang Wu, a bandit from Bailong Mountain, asked the monks to borrow silver. The monks refused. Jiang Wu said, "I will definitely take your gourd away within three days. Don't regret it." After Jiang Wu left, there were many monks in the temple with good skills. They watched him every day. On the third day, like a bird passing by, the gourd was lost. The monks chased after him in a group. After several miles, only two monks caught up. They fought, but there was no victory or defeat. Jiang Wu was tired and abandoned the gourd in the river. The two monks were ashamed and did not return. Today, there are still many skilled fighters in the temple, and the head monk of the kitchen is the most skilled. The temple makes and sells medicinal wine, which can cure madness and is quite effective.

Hong Jingshan's Poems 181

Solitary Night

A solitary night's mood connects to the distant and indistinct. I idly count the shooting stars through the pearly blinds. The lamp's flame flickers as if smiling. The rain on the eaves murmurs incessantly. I only lament that the fragrant blossoms are fading into twilight. Secretly, I add my own haggardness to the loneliness. The dawn bell shatters the moon through the gauze window. The quiet words still trouble me, listening in my dreams.

The New Year's scene is adorned with plum blossoms. His heart's devotion to repaying kindness reveres the distant India. The clouds of dedication connect to Potalaka. Don't say that enlightenment comes before or after. The supreme vehicle ultimately belongs to the white bullock cart.

Roman Art Study Notes (I) 182

— Wang Yachen

This time, I am studying the new and old art of Italy. In late April, I first arrived in Milan from Switzerland. I viewed Vinoi's famous work "The Last Supper." Then, from Milan, I went to Florence. From Florence, I passed through various scenic spots and finally arrived in Rome. I spent two weeks in Rome, enjoying daily excursions. The abundance of historical relics is truly the best in the world. Ancient Rome's artistic prosperity had reached its peak. Although the culture of various European countries originated in Greece, it was first transplanted to Rome, forming a major characteristic of ancient Roman stone architecture. As for religious art, it can be said that it all originated in Rome. It reached a special glory during the Renaissance in the fifteenth century. Therefore, the relics left today truly allow us to explore endlessly. I will briefly record the relics of Rome below.

(1) St. Paul's Cathedral: Rome has more than three hundred churches. The largest are St. Peter's and St. Paul's. This church is magnificently built. Its dome can be seen from a distance. Outside the church is a large open space. The space is surrounded by one hundred and twenty marble pillars. This church was destroyed by fire sixty years ago. It was rebuilt after the fire. It has been fifty years since its completion. The interior of the church is entirely inlaid with colored marble. There are many mosaics made of small colored marble squares. The religious paintings displayed in the church are mosaics made from Raphael's famous works, which are the same color as the original paintings. The precision of the inlay work is unparalleled. The dome and surrounding areas of the church's main hall are also inlaid with fine stones, including portraits of past great clergy. The pupils of one statue of St. Paul are made of diamonds. Looking up, their light shines in all directions. According to those in the know, the windows installed throughout the hall used eighteen trillion lire. (An Italian currency, each lira equals 14 cents in Chinese currency.) The spaces between the windows are made of thin slices of five-colored marble instead of glass. The stone is thin and translucent when exposed to light. The stone grain is fully exposed. The natural patterns of the stone grain are utilized, and each piece has a different pattern. Countless amounts of marble were used to obtain the patterns for these windows at the time. Roman church architecture spares no expense. It only seeks exquisiteness. Therefore, everything displayed inside the church is a precious work of art.

Warmth on My Mind (297) 183

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Fifteen: Tears Shed in All Directions, Mourning Red Affection; Hearts Enthralled in One Place, Lingering Green Sentiment

Let's talk about Zuo Shichen in the Emerald Bamboo Dressing Pavilion. Holding a crab and facing chrysanthemums, he was listening to Emerald Bamboo tell the tragic history of her little sister, Hong Lianxiang, after she married. To know the ins and outs of something, even when people came to urge Emerald Bamboo to sing her turn, he wouldn't let her go. He said it wouldn't be too late to go on stage after she finished telling the whole story. If you were in a hurry, you could have her tell it simply. But that Miss Emerald Bamboo was good at narrating. When she told a story, she had to start from the beginning, not omitting any details. People say, "To talk about burning a cloth shirt, you have to start from planting cotton." That Emerald Bamboo girl was much like this. Now, she was talking about that Mrs. Yin. Taking advantage of the master not being at home, she interrogated the coachman, Gengsheng. She thought Gengsheng was the person closest to the master. Wherever the master went, Gengsheng went. There couldn't be any mistakes. It was like finding a pearl in the mud. The other day, he inadvertently let out the words "the First Madam." That was the biggest loophole. She caught him then and asked him. Although he argued strongly, his face was already flushed red. It was obvious that he was being evasive. It was like examining examination papers, slowly examining them to find the problems. Haste doesn't make waste. If you pursue it too quickly, things might change. So she let him off then. Three or four days later, the master really did go out. As soon as the master went out, Gengsheng had a lot more free time. So the madam called him in and calmly questioned him. Like writing an essay, she first flattered him. If that method didn't work, she would use another method. Who knew that Gengsheng was ultimately a simple man? Mrs. Yin flattered him, and he came out with it. He even blamed his master in his heart. Why was he so honest? He told people not to reveal it, but he himself told the madam. In fact, Gengsheng had been tricked. Saying there was no Third Madam was like admitting that there was a Second Madam. He even thought he was smarter than his master. Mrs. Yin saw that this flattery had been effective. She then used the skill of oblique attacks. It's a pity that today's prosecutors didn't send an apprenticeship invitation to Mrs. Yin. They would definitely benefit greatly. Generally, to question someone and get a confession, you can't do it with carelessness and impatience. As for the interrogations of detectives, they are even more like blindly sticking needles, only causing people to suffer more. If you ask slowly, you will eventually get the truth. That day, the madam also said, "The master has already agreed to move the Second Madam into the mansion. It will probably be implemented after the master returns, after the confinement period. We have to clear out a room. I wonder if she has a lot of furniture." When the madam said this, she thought that since the master had taken a mistress outside, it must be mahogany furniture, foreign furniture. Needless to say, a lot of money must have been spent. So she tested Gengsheng's tone. As long as he said the furniture was more or less, it would prove that she had bought furniture. Who knew that Gengsheng only answered with a few "yes"s, not continuing the sentence.

Long-Term News Summary 187

Recently, it is the time for the expiration and replacement of long-term funds. Yesterday's news: (1) In the Ningbo financial community, the number of long-term funds deposited in Shanghai for lending is very high, estimated to be more than 20 million. According to the usual practice, they must continue to be made. In this session, because the deposits of each village are crowded, especially in Fenghua, there are even more deposits. Therefore, this long-term loan not only has no possibility of being collected, but instead has a huge increase. According to investigations from various aspects, the total amount will reach 30 million. (2) The total amount of funds expiring yesterday was about 7 million. More than half of the accounts transferred funds for several days. The specified interest price ranged from 8.5 to 10.05, among which the interest price varied due to the account's quality and different gangs. (3) More than 1 million of the expired funds of various domestic gangs were recovered, tens of thousands of were transferred, and tens of thousands were made in new transactions. The interest rate was around 9. (4) The expired amount of the Hankou gang was also several million. A general agreement has been reached that most of them will transfer accounts, but the interest rate will be determined when it expires. (5) For long-term deposits, old accounts are mostly transferred. New transactions are secretly traded with each other, so the outside world rarely knows. However, the total amount is even larger and cannot be estimated.

A Week's Observation of the Yarn Market 192

Raw Yarn... Environmental Deterioration Offers No Force for Price Increase

Spot Yarn... Demand is Quiet, Thick with Pessimistic Color

Last week, cotton yarns and actual sales became increasingly sluggish, with no vitality in any sector. This was due to financial weakness, resulting in weak purchasing power across all groups, coupled with the sluggish state of the global economy, leading to stagnant transactions. While many held an optimistic view of the situation, hoping for an improvement in demand, the prolonged war has depleted the vitality of various localities, making a swift recovery difficult. Furthermore, rampant banditry has deterred any excitement among various groups, resulting in an abnormally depressed market. The Chaozhou group and Japanese merchants showed a strong inclination to sell off their holdings. However, one factory bucked the trend and purchased a significant volume when prices fell. Nevertheless, it is difficult for a lone tree to support a tilting building against the prevailing trend. In summary, sluggish actual demand and the weakness of the global cotton industry indicate no potential for active price increases in the future. Japanese merchants are inclined to sell off raw yarn, and although some manufacturers are buying, the market continues to decline under such circumstances. Prices for all months have fallen by two to one and seven or eight mace (a unit of currency) compared to last week. The total transaction volume for the week was 120,700 bales, with spot yarn purchases by various groups amounting to 6,440 bales. The market price for Japanese 10-count "Blue Phoenix" yarn fell by two to three taels. If spot yarn sales do not improve, a major price drop may be in the offing, as its price is higher than futures contracts, and factories are offering very little.

A Glimpse of the Cotton Market During the Past Week 193

Chinese Standard Cotton Lacks Vitality... Prices for All Months Fall Again by Seven or Eight Mace

The Stillness of Spot Sales... Rare in Recent Years

At the beginning of the week, the cotton market trend had somewhat stabilized due to talk of a bailout for American cotton. Japanese merchants sold short, but after the meeting yielded no results, American cotton fell again, increasing anxieties. The Japanese firm, Toyo Cotton, resumed large-scale sell-offs, creating a sharp downward trend in the market. Actual spot cotton trading has been virtually eliminated, completely overtaken by Indian and American cotton. Furthermore, foreign firms are actively seeking solutions, willing to make special price concessions. With the retreat of bandits and the return of troops in Shashi, Hubei, transportation has become safer, and the influx of new cotton into Wuhan is gradually increasing, causing prices to fall by two yuan. Some in the Shashi group are hedging sales, while some retail investors, seeing the deteriorating situation, are cutting their losses. Consequently, prices for all months have fallen below the 31-tael mark. It is observed that many inland groups and the Tongzhou group, considering the poor local harvests, have brought in a significant volume of bales that have yet to be released, suggesting further significant changes in the future. According to veteran cotton merchants, the current cotton business is the quietest it has been in years, mainly because Chinese cotton is two to three taels more expensive. Therefore, both Chinese and foreign factories are purchasing Indian cotton for delivery in January, February, and March of next year, totaling approximately 200,000 to 300,000 pieces (each piece weighing 500 pounds). The future of the cotton market is not optimistic. Standard cotton prices for all months have fallen by seven or eight mace compared to last week. Total transaction volume for the week was 357,400 dan (a unit of weight). The sources at the dock were 10,000 bales of Yao cotton and 550 bales of Tong cotton. Factories purchased 72,824 dan of spot and futures cotton, and trading firms purchased 7,405 dan. The volume of purchases by various manufacturers and firms is listed below:

Fluctuations in U.S. Cotton Last Week 194

A New York dispatch from the 17th reports on the cotton market during the past week, stating that it was uneven and unpredictable. However, the underlying sentiment remained stable, as traders and speculators were buying the December futures contract below 15 cents. The maintenance plan discussed by the related groups at the New Orleans meeting on Monday has reportedly decided to advise yarn factories to immediately cover their long-term needs and advise banks to provide loans to secure their current cotton harvest and subsidize future production, with plans to reduce cotton planting next spring. It is also reported that the cooperative association will hold onto its 1.3 million bales in anticipation of a good price. These developments are somewhat encouraging, but have failed to stimulate recent demand. Yesterday's first frost had little impact on the market. The attached weekly statistics are listed below:

Grains: The Rice Market in Hexia Plummets 196

Zhabei: Yesterday, over fifty boats arrived from various groups on Luli Road, and market sales continued to worsen. Total rice inventory on the river reached as many as two hundred boats. New japonica rice fell by 40 cents, with premium grades opening particularly low at 15 yuan, and general grades also fell to 60-70 cents. Inferior grades were only offered at 12.8 yuan. Hanzhou rice was scarce and held steady. The market situation for xiang rice was uniquely stable due to sudden transactions from out-of-town buyers, combined with the reluctance of sellers to sell, thus enabling the market price to stand firm, opening high at 11.2 yuan for premium Dujian, with sources seeing immediate acceptance, and very active selling, with a small price decrease of about 40 cents. The overall price was 11.6 yuan. Port tip rice fell by 50 cents, only opening at 10.08 yuan. The market situation was unusually soft. Although inventory of Bianyuan rice was not high, there was an appearance of no buyers for available goods due to the lack of principals. The price of Yinyuan rice opened slightly higher, with high-grade goods at 13.3-13.4 yuan.

Hunan, Shanghai: Yesterday, about 30 boats arrived at the river. Sales in this district have collapsed. Changbang new japonica rice has fallen to 14.6 yuan. Sutong baijing rice is already on the left side of the 13 yuan level, with the price falling sharply. The inventory of bottom-grade rice in this district is increasing daily, with sluggish sales, hence the collapse. Southern rice varieties, such as thin-grained rice and white rice, were scarce, with frequent imports from Ningbo, and prices remained flat, opening at 13.5 yuan. Sheep Dujian rice was short by 20 cents, with prices ranging from 11 yuan to 9.5 yuan, with very little trading. The price of Bianyuan rice remained flat, and the price of Linghua rice fell slightly by 10 cents. The overall market situation showed a downward trend.

Flour Market Suddenly Tightens 197

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for all months suddenly showed signs of tightening. This was because the market had fallen sharply step by step during the previous week, which seemed excessive. The amount of imported wheat was limited, and the current atmosphere was entirely due to fixed orders, resulting in this panic. As for the factories' spot goods, they consistently held at the 2.3 mace level because the cost was high and there was no room for price cuts. Yesterday, due to factory purchases and slight activity from out-of-town buyers, the market recovered. A large number of floating long positions in the distant months have all been sold out, and the current buyers are all new players. With the market renewed, the sentiment also followed suit. As a result, the current month rose by 2.75 cents compared to the previous week, November to February rose by 2.5 cents, and March rose by 2.75 cents.

Wheat Futures Rebound Strongly 198

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning, the prices for all months remained flat because there was no change in the price of imported wheat. However, after the second session, the market secretly tightened because the current month must be delivered soon, and the inventory at the exchange was reported to be around 500 tons. The long side generally had preparations for receiving the goods, while the short side had no definite indication due to the commodity situation. Therefore, the sentiment suddenly rose, and the rebound was unusually strong. The sharp decline inevitably triggered the emergence of new long positions, and this cycle may be considerable in the future. November also jumped sharply due to the spot situation. As a result, the current month rose by 6 cents compared to the previous week, November rose by 1 qian, December rose by 5 cents, January and February rose by 6 cents, and March rose by 7 cents. The spot wheat market was improving, and the sentiment was also good. Special high-grade goods opened at 4.6 taels, while medium and lower-grade goods remained below the 4-tael mark. A total of 1,200 bags of high-grade Gaoyou, Bengbu, and Shandong wheat were purchased by Fufeng and Xinda.

Soybean Prices Rise Sharply 199

Yesterday, the standard soybean market was excellent, with strong buying interest from all parties, especially from factories. Short covering was also very active, so after receiving the report of rising prices from Dalian in the afternoon, the sentiment became more intense, and the price rose steadily. At closing, the December contract rose by 8 cents compared to last Saturday, and the January, February, and March contracts were all better by half. Spot soybeans opened flat in the morning, but the situation was lively in the afternoon, with Dalian Yuan soybeans quoted at 4.9 taels and Jiujiang late soybeans quoted at 4.978 taels, totaling 2,000 bags, which were purchased by Xiaomo and other groups.

(Pepper) Yesterday, a dispatch from Holland reported that the production market saw its price rise sharply by 6.75 guilders due to major hoarding purchases. Furthermore, seed farmers were unwilling to sell urgently, so there may be continued price increases in the future. The local trading firms, upon receiving this dispatch, tightened their holdings and tried to sell at higher prices. Moreover, the Huguang and Fujian groups' daily demand was quite strong. It is estimated that the number of transactions within this week was about 400 bags, so the inventory on the street gradually thinned. Sales in the northern provinces are also about to start. If there is no source of supply, there is a risk of demand exceeding supply, so the trading plate called for a rise in the price of black large original pepper to 52 taels per thousand, and No. 1 pepper to 51 taels, a rise of over 5 taels compared to the previous plate. Rice Market 210

Hu Nan

Yesterday, in the Hu Nan Rice Market, various gangs had 30 to 40 boats arriving. Transactions on this street were extremely light, and the market prices were gradually declining. Thick rice fell by 4 to 5 jiao, while other goods fell by 1 to 2 jiao. Only kiln seeds remained stable.

Shanghai Market

Organization News 219

The Shuguang English Study Morning School announces: Our school has been in preparation for several months and is now fully arranged. It officially opened on the 13th of this month, with classes from 7:00 to 8:30 AM. The curriculum includes business correspondence, bookkeeping, conversation, news, etc., all of which are practical. To reduce the financial burden on students, regardless of advanced or beginner level, the tuition fee is generally one yuan per month. Those who are interested should immediately report to the following address. There are not many places available, so please do not miss this opportunity. A prospectus is available, and will be sent upon request with a one-cent postage stamp. The school address is located in the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company on the 4th floor, No. 451 Jiangxi Road.

Wedding Record 220

Mao Heyuan, the general manager of Huashang Liying Western Medicine Store at No. 24 on the Bund, married Zhou Wenlin's daughter, Xiuying, at the Ningbo Fellow Association on Xizang Road at 3:00 PM yesterday. The introducers were Shen Hongkui and Zhu Jiliang, and the officiant was Yuan Ludeng. More than 500 guests attended, including Wang Xiaolai, Gu Zipan, Xie Zhongsheng, Sun Meitang, Xu Qingyun, Lu Shaotang, Zhang Shichuan, Gao Yongqing, Huang Yichang, and Le Zhenbao. The scene was bustling and grand. The gifts from celebrities were dazzling and beautiful. For example, Wang Zhengting, the Minister of Foreign Affairs, and Jiang Jieqing, the elder brother of Chairman Jiang, both presented flower baskets and other gifts. After the wedding ceremony, Chen Liangyu, Fang Jiaobo, and Yuan Ludeng gave speeches on behalf of the guests. Their remarks were both serious and humorous, moving the audience. Yesterday was also Mr. Mao's 40th birthday, so even more relatives and friends came to congratulate him. In the evening, there was a theatrical performance at the Shenshang Club, with programs including "Zhang Xian Delivers a Son," "Doing Good Deeds Brings a Son," "Opening Mountain Amulet," "Three Legs Standing," "Golden Terrace," "Happy Marriage," "Longevity Star," "Jade Hall Spring," "Xinglong Meeting," "Scolding the Palace," "Pearl Curtain Village," "Imperial Stele Pavilion." The wedding banquet was catered by Mr. Mao's own Meiyuan Restaurant, so the dishes were exceptionally delicious.

Chen Bingqian, a giant in the construction industry, has a talented son named Qixue, a graduate of Fudan University, with outstanding literary talent and elegant demeanor. Yesterday, he married Ms. Qian Jinhua at the Far Eastern Hotel Hall on Xizang Road. The guests filled the hall, all of whom were famous figures and business tycoons in Shanghai, making it a grand occasion. In addition, famous Shanghai opera singers Jiang Yingqiao, Rong Boming, Ms. Huang Fengyi, Yan Xiaolu, Sun Shaoyun, Wang Zhenbai, and others jointly performed Peking Opera. The amateur performers wore elaborate makeup and their performances were excellent. As a result, the traffic in front of the venue was extremely busy.

Market News 221

Qihua Company on Nanjing Road announces that the bustle of this company's price reduction in various departments is unprecedented, due to the complete variety of goods and affordable prices. The discounted section in the silk and satin department sells printed wool crepe for only 58 cents per foot. Newly arrived new floral velvet is discounted by 15%. Such a large-scale clearance sale is rare in the market. Gentlemen and ladies from all walks of life should not miss this opportunity.

Liangchen Good Friends Society at the intersection of Beijing Road and Zhejiang Road announces that it has been known for its artistic printing and enjoys a long-standing reputation. To facilitate customers viewing samples first, we have specially prepared letterhead and business card samples, with as many as forty or fifty pieces, so that you can choose paper materials, fonts, layouts, and printing colors to have a clear idea before ordering. Buying Liangchen letterhead now also gets the standard case. Those who wish to obtain it can send four cents in postage stamps.

Hongxing Dog Head Brand Sock Factory on Wuma Road announces that it is holding a special grand sale for fourteen days in celebration of its 12th anniversary. All Dog Head Brand silk, wool, and yarn socks, knitted goods, wool sweaters, health shirts, uniquely designed children's clothing, Western-style shirts, and this brand's insulated thermos bottles, and various European and American felt hats and children's hats (all of the above items are discounted by 10% during the sale period). Other goods are also sold at very low prices (and a large batch of seconds are also on sale). Genuine silk women's socks are three pairs for one yuan, genuine silk men's socks are two pairs for one yuan, cashmere wool socks are three pairs for one yuan sixty cents, double-thread socks are five pairs for one yuan, new floral children's socks are ten pairs for one yuan, and Western woolen blankets are two yuan and fifty cents each. This is truly an unprecedented great undertaking. Those who come to buy are extremely crowded.

Those named "eagle" are produced in the north, and those named "sea blue" are produced in the North Sea, which is the "tiger eagle" mentioned in the herbal medicine book "Compendium of Materia Medica." Youth Garden

Night Tour of Wusong—Mid-Autumn Festival 226

— Guangmei

"Brother, today is my seventh Mid-Autumn Festival away from home. Seven years ago today, I was still an innocent child, not fully understanding anything. No matter how busy Mother was with her affairs, or how urgently she was collecting debts, I couldn't and didn't know how to share the burden for her. I still happily played with you, piling up pastries, arranging toys, buying lanterns, decorating the Guanghan Palace to celebrate the Moon Goddess, and indulging in the golden rule of 'no moon indoors, rain and snow outdoors.' So, we competed to wash our hands and faces, devoutly worshiped the moon, and the firecrackers and incense filled the air. Do you remember this scene? It was this very night, wasn't it? You were all asleep, and Mother, exhausted from the day's work, had also gone to bed early. Only my older sister and I were still awake. So, without Mother's permission, we rashly went with our uncle and others to stroll around the city walls, going up from the South Gate and down to the North Gate. By the time we got home, the moon had already set, and our shoes and socks were soaked with dew. Coincidentally, Mother woke up and asked us where we had been. Not knowing the consequences, I proudly told Mother, only to find her extremely angry. She gave us a severe scolding, 'Girls in their teens have no reason to go out to play in the middle of the night. If we run into acquaintances, wouldn't they scold me for raising my children without any discipline?' My older sister secretly blamed me for being too straightforward and not leaving anything out. In fact, Heaven, how could I have known that she would be so furious, let alone that it was wrong to go? At the time, I hated Mother, 'Why can't girls go out to play in the middle of the night?' From joy came sorrow, and I could only resort to crying. My older sister did the same. Ah, brother, that was seven years ago. Now, now... It's unbearable to look back on the past, and the future is unpredictable.

Although I rationally know that I shouldn't care about the Mid-Autumn Festival, at this moment, reason can't overcome emotion. This subconscious, deeply rooted nature is a mystery even to myself. It's still morning now, and I'm already thinking like this. Today, today, how will I spend this moonlit night?"

Indeed, it was too much. I lost my reason and impulsively wrote the above passage and mailed it to my brother. I wonder what he'll think, whether he'll laugh at me for being old-fashioned or whether he's thinking of our parents too.

Of the sisters in the room, only Ye and I are left. The exceptionally bright moon shines through the window screen, directly illuminating the front half of the room. Because we love her so much, we temporarily turned off the lights. Ye and I stood facing the window, sighing frequently as if by agreement, "I'm so sad, so sad."

"I want to cry, Ye, but I hate that my tears are as precious as gold, not following my wishes."

"I want to cry too, crying seems to be pleasant, but I can't do it, so I won't cry."

We were silent for a while, and the whole room was filled with the feeling of travelers missing their families. The sacred moonlight enveloped this bitter feeling, making it seem even more desolate. A cricket, having lost its youth and vitality, was clearly making a final struggle, stammering intermittently, as if to help the travelers express their unbearable grief. We were even more saddened.

"Ah, beautiful moon, how bright you are. Tonight, tonight is my seventh Mid-Autumn Festival away from home. Kind Mother, adorable younger siblings, do they, do they still remember me at this moment? Recalling the scene of strolling around the city walls seven years ago, at that time, the ignorant me hated Mother. Now..."

When Xiu in the opposite room heard my voice, she hurriedly ran over excitedly, "Haha, Guangmei is making a new drama again." Her words interrupted my thoughts. At the same time, I realized that life is actually not that different from acting in a play. Precious tears fell without restraint and weren’t valuable in the slightest.

"Ah, Guangmei, you're crying. If you cry, I'll cry too," Ye was the first to notice.

"You're lucky you can cry, like little kids. I'm not sad at all. If I miss home, I'll miss my friends," Xiu said without sympathizing with us, making us even sadder.

"If you miss friends, it doesn't necessarily have to be tonight. There's only the saying 'people miss their loved ones all the more during festivals,' there's no reason to miss friends all the more," Ye argued with her while still laughing. I didn't want to say anything, and collapsed on the bed, sobbing to myself.

"Get up, Guangmei, don't cry. Crying is a sign of weakness, it's shameful. Useless youths, let's try to enjoy the moon. Don't waste this good night," Ye said, clearly using reason to restrain her emotions.

"Okay, okay, besides working hard, what else can we say? Let's go have fun. Don't waste this good night."

As a result of our discussion, we decided to go to Paotaiwan. But that would be too monotonous. To be honest, we were a little scared. We planned to call Mao in Wusong to go with us.

"Where are you going?" Shen and Zhuang asked us as they met us.

"Nowhere in particular, and you?" Ye and I replied in unison.

"Is Wusong good to go?"

"Extremely good. That's what we were thinking too."

"Okay, let's go together."

Shen and Zhuang had to wait for half an hour at the Wusong station while Ye and I asked Mao to come over. At the time, I could only apologize profusely to Shen and Zhuang. Words were simply not enough to express the apology I felt.

Paotaiwan was nothing like it usually was. The narrow roads were packed with people, and it was hard to get through. Clearly, people were still reluctant to let go of the lunar Mid-Autumn Festival. Along the way, residents had set out many seasonal foods and fruits to celebrate the Moon Goddess. The sounds of stringed instruments and firecrackers were all mixed together. It was clear that the lunar calendar was difficult to abolish quickly.

"Guangmei, Meiguang," A lively expression filled a clear voice. Clearly, it was a woman's voice. I was pleasantly surprised. "Who's calling me?" Although the voice was very familiar to me, I couldn't guess who it was right away. Taking a closer look,

"Ah, Tang, is that you? I didn't even notice. How many of you came?" I excitedly shook her hand.

"Guangmei," Again a voice very familiar to me. Tang hurriedly told me "It's Mr. Li." I was extremely happy to also meet Mr. Li Tianxing, a teacher I respect. Then, Comrade Deng greeted me. They were gathered on the Qing dike, a large rock that jutted out between the Huangpu River and the Yangtze River, eating things, probably with alcohol as well, enjoying their elegant moon viewing event.

We moved forward along the rugged stone road. Gradually, there were no pedestrians ahead and no one coming behind. But we were still very far from the lighthouse. So, we stopped and took a break. This abandoned dike has the Huangpu River on its left and the Yangtze River on its right, with the lighthouse in front. The Huangpu River surged fiercely, while the Yangtze River was quiet and serene. The universe is just such a symbol. The Huangpu is like a brave and well-mannered knight, while the Yangtze is like a gentle and sweet beauty. The strong knight smashed the round moon into pieces, and we saw streaks of golden light, dazzling. Far, far away, farther, straight out to where the water and sky could not be distinguished, it seemed as if the golden earth covered the surface of the river. Mr. Shen, however, would tease Mr. Zhuang from time to time, "Zhuang, look, how many moons are in the water?" We also threw stones into the water. The stones over there weighed at least a few pounds. Ye and I, however, put in all our might, which is a shame to say, but they still supplied us the rocks. We couldn't reach to get the stones ourselves. Their strength was greater, so the stones they threw were bigger, and the sound was louder. The meaning of life is just this. It's like a thrown stone being able to make ripples on the surface of the water, which has some influence on mankind. What's more, the stones we threw down make a loud sound.

It was already 9:30. We started to turn back. By the time we walked back to the dike, the tourists had dispersed almost entirely. Tang and Mr. Li and the others had left before us at some point. We talked and walked until we reached the station, and it was already 10:30. I was only worried about whether Mao would be able to get back to school on time. Before long, Wusong Town was here, and Mao said goodbye to us.

After getting off at Tiantong'an, in order to not waste the good moonlight, we simply walked to school. The firm moonlight filled the earth. There wasn't a single pedestrian on the smooth, dance-hall-like Jiangwan Road. Only the reflections from the asphalt ground, shining brightly, illuminated us. I didn't know if they were welcoming us or seeing us off. I said happily to Guang, "Jiangwan Road is ours, look, there isn't a single pedestrian. You precious poet, this is exactly the time for you to write a poem. The earth has already presented you with a firm poetic intention."

When we arrived at the school, the clock tower told us it was a quarter to twelve. We were too careless. But it was truly a once-in-a-lifetime phenomenon.

Daxia Wanbai Literary Society 227

Recently, literary groups in various universities have been growing and flourishing like bamboo shoots after a spring rain. Especially the newly emerging Daxia in Huxi, this semester has more than 1,700 students and has natural beauty. So, from the beginning of school until now, only a month, various social organizations have already sprung up, and the well-performing Wanbai Literary Society, in order to promote fellowship among its members and advance the society's affairs, held a general meeting of all members at the school's church No. 212 on the 14th of this month. The society's membership has almost doubled compared to last semester, totaling about a hundred people. Yesterday's general meeting, except for those who were absent due to affairs, about eighty people attended, gathered together, and it was a grand occasion. When the bell rang seven times, the meeting was officially announced. Then, Mr. Xu Zexiang was publicly elected as the chairman of the meeting, and Mr. Zhang Zhenyong was the record keeper. First, Mr. Xu Zexiang gave the opening remarks, and the intention was new and outstanding. The entire hall's atmosphere became even more tense. Then, the previous executive committee members gave reports on their work. The whole body was also quite satisfied with the report. Then, the guidelines for the society's operations and the amendments to the charter were discussed in succession. Then, new and old members were introduced. Then, elections were held again. The results of the election were Xu Zexiang, Ms. Hu Kewen, Zhang Zhenyong, Xie Shufu, Wang Ruinian, Tong Shiquan, Geng Kangfu, and ten other members. After the election, the amusements began, and the atmosphere was raised. For example, Mr. Cheng Chunlin's English song, Pan Quan, Mei Guangdao, and others' Peking Opera and Kunqu Opera, all received a lot of applause. After a heated congress, it adjourned at ten thirty o'clock. (Also, Qiu)

Autumn Rain Night (Reading) 228

— Zhen

"Nationalistic literature has a very deep and solid foundation in the world's documents, from Greece to the present. This history is described in great detail in the "Declaration of the Nationalist Literary Movement." You can read it carefully yourself. In short, the facts must be based on evidence. The nationalist literary movement is not without basis. Moreover, it is us! Not just us—we should come out and do this kind of movement. There is also a very powerful fact proving the urgent need for the nationalist literary movement. According to the latest surveys of unemployed populations in various countries around the world, the United States has 5 million unemployed, the United Kingdom has 3 million, Japan has 1 million, and China? It is impossible to count. Even worse than unemployment, there are about 80 million people who cannot even find bark and grass roots to eat. The unemployed workers in the United States, the United Kingdom, and Japan are only 5 million, 3 million, or 1 million, but it has already caused a great uproar, and the government is racking its brains to find relief methods. But what about China? I am afraid that unemployment will only wait for the time when there is no food to eat, and those who have to eat bark and grass roots will probably have no hope other than waiting for death. In such suffering, what other way is there but to carry out thorough relief based on nationalism to achieve the goal of self-determination? Therefore, the nationalist movement, using facts to prove it, is the urgent task at hand."

Rong's words were like this. Therefore, his efforts in the nationalist literary movement were what he should do. However, continuing to work tirelessly like this would inevitably harm his weak body. From my standpoint and in the circle of love, I cannot abandon my sincerity in caring for him and gently persuade him to rest on time at fixed rest hours every night. Therefore, I helped him while also advising him to rest on time.

This was truly beyond my expectations. Before 5 o'clock this afternoon, Brother Rong leisurely returned home from the office. At this time, the maid had not yet washed the rice to prepare for cooking. I was afraid that he had already been tired all day and was about to start writing again, so I begged him to go to a restaurant—begged him to go to Sinya to eat Nanyang Curry Chicken. Getting his consent, we went to Sinya.

Sinya, this Cantonese restaurant, was originally where we often ate before we got married. Rong also often went there with his friends to drink tea and eat dim sum. Moreover, at one time, many of Rong's literary works were produced there. According to him, Sinya has a special charm for him, and he has an excellent impression of Sinya. Everything there makes him feel very satisfied. As for why I like it, of course, it is because it is truly both new and elegant, and I also love to eat its Nanyang Curry Chicken the most, because this dish is particularly delicious at Sinya. Other restaurants can't compare, not to mention what you can cook at home. We arrived at Sinya at five minutes before half-past five. Rong was not happy to go to the third floor, so we chose a seat in the west hall on the second floor. Everything was familiar to us, and this time, unintentionally, we paid no attention to it at all. However, at the west end of two square tables put together to form a long table on the south side, a diner sitting there especially caught my attention. Of course, there was more than just him sitting on both sides of the table; there were several others. But he really made me pay too much attention. He was laughably fat, a stout, large lump like a German sausage, with a purplish-red face, filled with vulgarity. He held onto the corners of the table with both hands, one of which also raised his thumb, tearing open his lips, revealing his teeth, and chatting with his tablemates. He was speaking Cantonese, but it was Cantonese that we Cantonese people couldn't understand. His strange appearance made me guess that he was a henchman of some Cantonese gang, or the boss of a North-South grocery store. But Rong said that he was the Cantonese who was famous for writing triangular love novels. I couldn't help but laugh and say, "No wonder his fat face doesn't have a bit of elegance." Rong laughed when he heard this, and a bowl of Nanyang Curry Chicken, which we love to eat, had already been brought to the table by a waiter in white clothes.

Guidelines for Youth Garden Contributions 229

(1) The text should be within the scope of discussions on youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, and notes. The style is not limited.

(2) Books are limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Photos that qualify include youth life (such as sports, travel, sightseeing, drama performances, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Both individuals and groups are welcome.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

Book and Newspaper Reviews

"Youth Lamp" Inaugural Issue 230

— Gao Wei

Edited by the Youth Lamp Society

Distributed by Daguang Bookstore

"Youth is the core of the times, the source of society, and the vitality of the nation. Everyone says this, but what exactly is the manifestation of the facts? Look, youth cannot awaken themselves to take on major responsibilities and missions, and various publications that point out the way for generally blind and clueless youth also lack a central consciousness and are equally pathetic. Therefore, youth in this situation naturally form a more and more chaotic phenomenon, further and further away from people's earnest expectations.

Since we youth are imbued with the vitality of the nation, then we should strive for our nation. Our nation is currently in an era of suffering, and the responsibility lies on the shoulders of us youth. How will youth extricate the nation from the whirlpool of suffering? Not long ago, we were very happy to discover a "Youth of the Times." This publication can be said to have risen suddenly in the youth world. Its consciousness is centered on the national movement, and it has been widely welcomed by the youth world since its publication. This also proves that youth themselves are increasingly entering a realm of awakening. However, this has unknowingly triggered a lively phenomenon in youth publications. Recently, we have also discovered this "Youth Lamp."

In the "Inaugural Statement," we can recognize that "Youth Lamp's" attitude is like this:

We know that the power to drive the times mostly relies on the efforts of the youth of the times. To put it more sharply and incisively, it can also be said that it completely relies on nurturing youth. I believe this statement may not be an overstatement in any way. Isn't the fact laid out before our eyes like this? Therefore, in recent times, the depression of youth's will and the recklessness of their actions have been followed by the depression of the will and the recklessness of the actions of the majority of the people. The entire nation has also become depressed and gone downhill, creating the current era of great terror on the verge of collapse.

For this reason, they dare not remain silent any longer. They want to sincerely do their best for youth, and so "Youth Lamp" was born in this way.

We know that our Chinese nation has many defects, and we should naturally actively think of ways to cure them, infuse the consciousness of the nation, and ignite the torch of the nation. To implement this plan, to trace the origin and explore the root, we should start by curing the sick bear of youth to save the core of the times. The colleagues know that knowledge and ability are both shallow, but seeing the imminent crisis, based on our inner selves, we always feel that we should do our best, exhaust our knowledge, erect the bright lamp of youth, point the way to the general youth wandering at the crossroads, and lead them to the wide road we yearn for.

What a huge responsibility this is! At the same time, the diseases of youth are so complex. Our small and weak cry cannot arouse the excitement of the times or awaken all the deluded youth. This is naturally expected. However, driven by our inner selves, we feel that we must light this street lamp. Therefore, "Youth Lamp" was born in this way.

But—the inaugural statement says this. Before seeing the content, we naturally cannot rashly believe it. So, let's examine the content before speaking.

Yang Shaozhi's "Respectfully Dedicated to Those in Charge of Student Organizations" is a text that prescribes the right medicine. The author first criticizes the actions of past student organization leaders, and then puts forward his three requirements. First, the officials of student-run associations should truly become public servants of all students to fulfill the expectations of those who entrust them. Second, in terms of thought, they should establish a correct consciousness and point out a correct path for students. They should do their best for the nation. Third, in terms of action, they should recognize the correct path and find a way out from the bright side. Alas, those in charge of student organizations in various schools, please ponder these three points more!

Tao Yuchuan's "Youth and Literature" explains the close relationship between youth and literature very clearly. At the end, the author points out that our literature should advance towards the road of national freedom.

The case of Locke "Not Afraid of Death" fills us with sorrow. Such a great shame to the nation, anyone with a slight sense of nationalism, will stand up to oppose it. But this kind of opposition is still passive. We must start from the positive aspects and engage in our own films. This is the good result of this stimulation. Xu Xiyu's "From the 'Not Afraid of Death' Incident to Nationalist Cinema" emphasizes this aspect and urges youth to deeply reflect. We know that film is developed by the combination of industry, science, and art. Film is the eighth art in the category of emerging arts. In modern times, we not only see the historical facts of national literature in literature and art, but the progress of world national literature is even more obvious. However, the evolution of nationalism in film is even stronger, especially in the aspect of national identity, it is expressed more clearly. Recently, the imperial

Page 24

ism toward weak nations, but using films, borrowing the expression of films to show the greatness of their own nation and the inferiority of other nations. Now "Not Afraid of Death" is exactly like this. Therefore, the author believes that Chinese films in the future should strive for the nationalist film movement.

In addition, there are also Shen Shuowen's "The Self-Awareness That Chinese Youth Students Should Have" and Tang Zeng's and Xu Zexiang's poems, etc. Xilun's "Scraps of School Life" is like chewing gum. Shaozhi's novel "The Death of a Warrior" depicts a scene of a warrior plotting an Indian national revolution. It is an unfinished manuscript, so there is nothing to say about it.

In general, this "Youth Lamp" has not yet made any major breakthroughs. If it continues to work hard to improve, it is not difficult to become a central publication in the youth world, standing in the same position as "Youth of the Times," encouraging and stimulating the national consciousness of youth, and urging youth to fulfill their due mission.

The Plants in This Garden Are Very Beautiful 231

— Gao Wei

What I want to introduce here is the crystallizing "Wuben" inaugural issue collected by Wuben students. But I must declare in advance that the title above borrows the words of You Xiang's "Last Page." You Xiang's intention is humility, afraid that people will praise him like this, so he says he can't afford it first, but I can't help but disagree. This, I should first ask You Xiang to forgive.

Generally speaking, women's works always have a special flavor. It's not arbitrary, especially works like this, which are really a great opportunity to study women's psychology. In the works, it seems as if the whole heart is exposed. Their hot blood, their emotions, everything in their hearts is nakedly expressed. Because there is no other concept existing in their hearts, they only have the memories of inherent scars, or the eulogy of youth, or expectations for their own future. Even if they express some dissatisfaction with the social reality environment, they only rely on ordinary concepts and there will be no violent conflicts. This is how life makes them (if you don't believe it, you can refer to the nearby "Wuben"). Therefore, the value of this kind of work that is worth our savoring is to make us recognize what kind of outline is forming in the hearts of a general new era of female students. Although it cannot be said that these are all harmonies of their hearts, there are more or less connotations of their subjective views. "We want to cry, we cry; we want to laugh, we laugh. Here, there are our tears, our laughter, our dreams, songs, our pity, anger, and sympathy." Isn't it more proving to read the words of "Wuben's" "First Page"?

On the other hand, because women are more sentimental by tradition, they may be more neurotic than men. The sad part of them, just talking about "tears," when we read Qi Ying's "Talking about Crying," it says that crying is a woman's special responsibility, which is more like speaking for herself.

In this lesson, I want to talk about the literary and artistic aspects specifically. Henglu's three-act play "Flattery, Snobbery" is cursing the flattery and snobbery of men, using bank clerks to vent their anger. There are indeed not a few stories about describing love stories. It's really worth seeing love. Cursing rituals and teachings, there are Nuzhen's "Peace," Qingqin's "Mad Woman," Yun's "Rebellious Prisoner," Er's "Dusk," Luo Meiyun's "Miss C," Ruolian's "A Letter," etc. We can recognize the women struggling under rituals and teachings. Alas, rituals and teachings are really the great enemies of youth! Ali's "Past" describes teacher-student love, and the teacher's hungry appearance is made to look like he wants to cry but can't laugh. Nuzhen's "Times Smaller Than Now" describes the situation of being drunk in love, and the psychology is indeed more clearly described than by men. In addition, there are several tragedies describing love. Yiyun's "Clear Breeze in the Bedroom" makes us laugh so much that we can't stop. I really thank this lady for revealing a fragment of life. This is Chun's conversation written before going to bed. We can know what kind of impression the general women's views on love leave in their hearts. Pin San's "Ornament" completely exposes the hypocrisy of men, implying that the general young men do not hesitate to please women and make themselves beautiful. They use other people's help to make money, but when it comes to women's social events, they put on enough airs, suits, cosmetics.

Others, in the fillers, there are also many that are mean to men, and at the same time, they also express their true feelings. For example, Luo Ying's one, two, and three-page filler, "All the women in the world are disasters." If a man thinks that this is "correct," then he can ignore near women."

As for those who tell their inner sorrow, there are also many, such as Ping's "Tears" and "Sorrow of Life," simply sighing "Life is really sad, life is really sad." The lamp in Pin San's Na Dengxia is also a piece of suffering, the sorrow for the passing of youth, there are really too many tears. Secondly, there are not a few who feel the troubles of youth. Here are examples of fillers, because I think fillers are more real. Nuzhen said on page two hundred and eighteen, "Such a life is too lonely for me. How can you not cry to me? God, since you have given me youth, why do you give me loneliness?" Oh, the passion is extreme.

There are several articles here that are written very meaningfully, and the text is also very beautiful, such as Zhixiao's "White Clouds," Ping's "Blood," Yiyi's "Village," and You Xiang's "String Sound," but I don't want to introduce them one by one, I'm afraid it will take up too much space.

Therefore, in general, if this "Wuben" can be infused with correct central ideas, it is really not difficult to become an excellent member of the nation. However, I hope that the students of "Wuben" should avoid the attitude of "wanting to cry and crying, wanting to laugh and laughing" in the future. Of course, this shows the purity of your hearts, but you must know that literary and artistic works cannot simply rely on personal consciousness to be unrestrained once. In the current rapid current of the times, on the one hand, we cannot forget the requirements of women's own liberation, and on the other hand, we cannot forget the responsibility for the nation and the country. Alas, let's not care too much about our own desires. We must create a bright road for our nation. We cannot live alone in an "ivory tower."

Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Review Contributions 232

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest domestic and foreign publications. In addition to literary and artistic works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc. books and newspapers are included in the introduction. However, boring books and newspapers will not be introduced.

(2) The pictures are limited to the latest works of domestic and foreign new writers and the attached pictures related to the text.

(3) Texts on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Pictures and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(5) Each text should not exceed three thousand words at most.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not write the manuscript horizontally, and do not write the characters in cursive. Western texts can be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached under the translation.
